  <script>
   switch(true) {
    case !!location.search.match('new_comments=false'):
      window.showNewComments = false;
      break;
    case !!location.search.match('new_comments=true'):
      window.showNewComments = true;
      break;
    case !!document.cookie.match('new_comments=false'):
      window.showNewComments = false;
      break;
    case !!document.cookie.match('new_comments=true'):
      window.showNewComments = true;
      break;
    case (true && DailyKos.isLoggedIn()):
      window.showNewComments = true;
      break;
    case (true && !DailyKos.isLoggedIn()):
      window.showNewComments = true;
      break;
    default:
      window.showNewComments = false;
  }
  </script>

        if (typeof DailyKos.currentStoryID != 'undefined') {
          _sf_async_config.sections = DailyKos.currentStoryTags.join(',');
          _sf_async_config.authors = DailyKos.currentStoryAuthor;

      }

  <script type="text/javascript">
   (function() {
    var _sf_startpt=(new Date()).getTime();
    var _sf_async_config = window._sf_async_config = (window._sf_async_config || {});
    _sf_async_config.uid = 2709;
    _sf_async_config.domain = String('dailykos.com');
    _sf_async_config.flickerControl = false;
    _sf_async_config.useCanonical = true;
    _sf_async_config.useCanonicalDomain = true;

    if(String("").toLowerCase() === "true") {
      _sf_async_config.sections = 'dk-action';
      _sf_async_config.authors = 'dk-activism';
    } else {
      if (typeof DailyKos.currentStoryID != 'undefined') {
        _sf_async_config.sections = DailyKos.currentStoryTags.join(',');
        _sf_async_config.authors = DailyKos.currentStoryAuthor;
      }
    }

    function loadChartbeat() {
      var e = document.createElement('script');
      var n = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
      e.type = 'text/javascript';
      e.async = true;
      e.src = '//static.chartbeat.com/js/chartbeat.js';
      n.parentNode.insertBefore(e, n);
    }

    loadChartbeat();
  })();
  </script>

   <script>
    if (DailyKos.Ads && DailyKos.Ads.isAdsPage()) {
    htlbid.cmd.push(function() {
      if (!!DailyKos.currentStoryID) {
        htlbid.setTargeting('story_id', DailyKos.currentStoryID);
        htlbid.setTargeting('groups', DailyKos.currentStoryGroupNames);
        htlbid.setTargeting('tags', DailyKos.currentStoryTags);
        htlbid.setTargeting('home', 'false');
      } else {
        htlbid.setTargeting('home', 'true');
      }
      htlbid.setTargeting('domain', window.location.hostname);
      htlbid.setTargeting('referrer', document.referrer);
      htlbid.setTargeting('pathname', window.location.pathname);
      htlbid.setTargeting('signed_petitions', DailyKos.Ads.getSignedPetitions());
      htlbid.setTargeting('last_splashed_datetime', DailyKos.Ads.getLastSplashed());
      htlbid.setTargeting('page_type', DailyKos.pageType || "");
    });
  }
   </script>
   <div class="htl-ad interstitial-ad hidden" data-eager="" data-oop="" data-unit="Interstitial_1x1">
    <script>
     if (DailyKos.showsAds() && $.browser.desktop) {
        DailyKos.Ads.push('.interstitial-ad');

        htlbid.cmd.push(function() {
          htlbid.on('slotRenderEnded', function(slot) {
            if(slot.adUnitPath == '/1095769/Interstitial_1x1') {
              $('.interstitial-ad')
                .find('iframe:first')
                .load(function() {
                  App.Ads.Splash.init({
                    $iframeContainer: $('.interstitial-ad'),
                    showAd: function () {
                      $('body').addClass('show-interstitial');
                      $('.interstitial-ad > div').css({height: '100%'});
                      $('.interstitial-ad > div > div').css({height: '100%'});
                    },
                    hideAd: function () { $('body').removeClass('show-interstitial'); },
                    onLoad: function () { }
                  });
                });
            }
          });
        });
      }
    </script>
   </div>
   <div class="htl-ad mobile-petition-ad hidden" data-eager="" data-sizes="1x1" data-unit="MOB_Petitions">
    <script>
     if (DailyKos.showsAds() && $.browser.mobile) {
        DailyKos.Ads.push('.mobile-petition-ad');

        htlbid.cmd.push(function() {
          htlbid.on('slotRenderEnded', function(slot) {
            if (slot.adUnitPath == '/1095769/MOB_Petitions') {
              var $iframeContainer = $('.mobile-petition-ad');
              var $iframe = $iframeContainer.find('iframe:first');

              $iframeContainer.addClass('hidden');

              $iframe.load(function() {
                App.Ads.Splash.init({
                  $iframeContainer: $iframeContainer,
                  showAd: function () {
                    $('.mobile-petition-ad').removeClass('hidden');
                  },
                  hideAd: function () {
                    $('.mobile-petition-ad').addClass('hidden');
                  },
                  onLoad: function () {
                    DailyKos.Ads.Google.addMobilePetitionEventListeners($iframe);
                  }
                });
              });
            }
          });
        });
      }
    </script>
   </div>
